et enmi les .ij. liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	and in between the .2. limbs are two adjustments of this same stalk, which are secured in one and the other, half a palm long or a little more;
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les .ij. cornes.	and these two adjustments are inserted in the mouth of the wound to open it when you turn the two horns.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, more subtle and lighter in appearance, is made of ebony wood or boxwood, according to the appearance of tweezers;
et ait as .ij. chiés .ij. ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et .ij. dois de large;	and it has two heads with two adjustments, as you can see, a palm long and two digits wide;
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor .i. lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes,	and when you see the wound open to all the instrument, then let the woman sit on a bed, her feet hanging and her legs spread apart,
puis boute les .ij. ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	then press the two incisions together in the wound, and hold the head of the instrument under between his buttocks;
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	then work your hand on the entire instrument, just as you did with the tongs, according to how much you want to open the mouth of the wound, until the patient does what he wants.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances; et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	These instruments are all tipped and have multiplied their appearances; and when the surgeon has prepared them, the work is faster and higher in men due to their quantity.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	Do not despair of the instrument that you have not prepared, for its necessity is inexcusable.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the afterbirth is retained at childbirth, you must instruct the patient to hold back her breath, then make her sneeze with some powder, and hold her hands over her mouth and nose.
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	And if she vomits, all the better.
Se ceu non, si prent .i. pot, et fai .i. pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If not, take a jar or vessel and put in it herbs that can open the mouth of the womb, such as chamomile, fennel, anise, and clary sage.
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu; puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris,	All these herbs, or some of them, should be cooked in water over the fire; then put one end into the jar's opening, and the other end into the mouth of the womb,
et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris; puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	and let the hairs grow until the vapors enter the wound; then make it sneeze, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	Then let the pus drain freely.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature,	And if it remains after this treatment and is not removed, then command the patient to moisten her left hand in oil of sesame or in musk-saturated olive oil, and then let her wave it around in the air.
et quiere la secondine; et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	and seek out the pus; and when she has found it, she should squeeze it gently little by little so that the wound is not pulled on;
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie; si venra et se desaerdra.	but it must be moved slightly to the right and left, and then pulled; it will come out and be cured.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the mouth of the wound is tight, we have described the cure through sneezing, and the fumigation of herbs;
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	and if it is not cured by all that we have said, then beware of pulling;
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	but it is necessary that he who is at the mouth of the wound, that you tie him to the thigh of the woman, then cleanse her with four-fold ointment;
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer; mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	if she will let it out and then put it back in, but nonetheless when she does this there comes a bad smell to the stomach and head, and it makes her ill.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu: aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	Therefore one should use suitable fumigations: some of the ancients have tried fumigation with watercress and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The instrument used to fumigate the woman for retained placenta and afterbirth is as follows:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	And it is made of glass like a pipe, with the narrow end inserted into the woman's body and the wider end placed over the fire;
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	and let there be fumigation over the coals, and the dye until it is exhausted, and then begin another.
de percier lou fondement	of piercing the foundation
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born who do not have their foundation pierced, but rather have a thin, subtle membrane.
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	so the midwife should pierce this membrane with her finger, and not with a sharp instrument, and guard against tying it too tightly so that it does not touch [the child].
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	then place on moist linen with wine and oil, then dress with ointment until healed.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt that it will heal, then place a wooden plug in the hole, and leave it for several days, and remove it when the child wants to go inside.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme; si covient coper celui soudement: si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	And sometimes the healing of a wound or abscess comes suddenly; so it must be covered suddenly: then it should be dressed, as we have said, with a plug of wood.
de la fistule dou fondement	from the fistula in the anus
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des .ij. parties,	Fistulas that come from under the anus are nodular and grow larger than those that originate elsewhere in the rectum or in the space of its two parts.
si a une fistule ou plusors; et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe,	If there is one or more fistulas; and when that nodule is old, it opens and discharges moisture or pus and thin blood.si li cuitent li fondement, et l’un en l’auter costé del fese, et encort par le corps sus le quareix, si est grant mal, si li gaste li meisme cuit a l’auter costé del cuit.
et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans; et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	And sometimes these fistulas are piercing; and they are caused by what is in the digestion or wind when the patient makes an eruption, and by chance some of it emerges.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge; et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	And if there are fistulas that pierce up to the bladder, and up to halfway down the penis; and they reach up to the joint of the thigh, and up to the head of the cow.Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge; et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus one knows a fistula which is not bleeding from the anus, but which is still bleeding.
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	and you should push your index finger into the anus and insert a thin needle of bronze or iron into the fistula when there is no twisting.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou .i. poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	And if it is twisted, then you should insert a thin tent or horsehair into the fistula until you feel the tent or hair with your finger;
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	and if you do not feel it, and there is no discharge or farting or feeling of the fistula as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie; si te haste dou curer.	let it heal without piercing it; then you can dress it.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula has pierced to the bladder or the passage of urine, then the urine flows out and cannot be stopped by medicine.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If it has pierced to the hip joint, then the tent will feel wet at that spot.
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	If there is twisting and the pain extends around, then it will be better to let it drain without using any ointment or medicine.
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	and in these persian fistulas there is no cure but labor and the folly of those who interfere with it.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit,	In that which is not Persian and is not old, there is hope of healing by fire, as I have experienced.
et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos; et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	and the patient lies on his back with his legs stretched out to his thighs and his thighs sloping towards his belly.
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	Then insert a tent of bronze or lead, if there is tortuosity, as far as you know the tent comes.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice,	If the pain is felt around the anus, you must insert your index finger there.
se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet; et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	Then feel around with your finger until you perceive the hole; and if it is covered by skin or flesh, then know that it is perforated.
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	if one does not work on it, it cannot be healed.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	One can indeed heal some, but that rarely happens;
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	and the help that is given, one burns the cautery thinly according to the size of the fistula, as has been said before;
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement; et faice ceu .ij. fois ou .iij., tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	and insert it into the fistula as far as the anus; and do this two or three times until you know that the infected matter is burned, which will appear like the quill of a bird;
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	then treat with moist bandages soaked in butter until the infected matter comes out, and then apply ointment to heal and close the wound.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien. Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If it is healed like this, that is good. If not, then it cannot be healed otherwise;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	and if the tent is inserted, and does not pierce all the way to the bottom which is in the foundation, and there is between your finger and the tent a thick covering of flesh or of syphilis, and you see the fistula following the covering of the skin;
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	if you cut at the beginning of the fistula, and insert again before the tent, and then cauterize afterward, until it reaches the tip of the tent;
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra; puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	and the tent will be released and fall out; then cut off those false meats which look like a bird's feather, and nothing will remain.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if the pus runs, and cuts between your finger and the wound, then cauterize it with fire or with medicine.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble .ij. bones choses: c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	For fire cautery brings together two things: the charring of the flesh and the stemming of blood and the drying of moisture.
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	Then dress the wound with moist bandages or with crushed substances until the flesh heals and the scars fade.
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	Then treat the wound with ointments of soft fat, which is solid, and they are dry remedies.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is restored, it is healed and does not return.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if a fistula comes all the way from the anus, and is separated from the body, put your finger into it and probe it.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre .ij. est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des .iii. manieres:	If you feel the tent, and between the two is the foreskin or scrotum, or it is about to pierce, there should be no fear but hope, through the administration of one of three remedies:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	either you cauterize it as we have said, or you cut it to the bottom, or if you can, put in a tent and treat it as before.
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	And do not go too deep, lest you cut the tissue that holds the anus, and cause the evacuations to come out through there instead;
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	then heal, as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	by chance if it is healed, then remove that covering and wash it once the wound is cut away from the foundation, either by probing or by another pointed instrument;
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	then clean the wound as much as you can;
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement: si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	then examine how to heal the wound and keep the fistula in the part above the foundation: if there is something lighter for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere: et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus,	And sometimes they are fistulas according to this manner: it is when you tie a thread in the fistula, and it is on the side of the root of the skin above.
si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	take a thread pierced at the end according to this form:
Et i boute .i. fil tort en .ij., et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And he ties .a. twisted thread in ii, and ties the thread all the way into the fistula until it reaches the root.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it is piercing on the margin of the root inside, then pull out the thread from that hole as you would when you put your finger into the root;
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les .ij. chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse .i. jor ou .ij.;	and draw the head of the thread, and gather the two heads together, and hold one against the other, and let it rest for one or two days;
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	and restrain it sometimes, until the threads catch the hairs that are between two;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	then heal the wound until it is closed and healed.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not drain, then have it drained in every way you can, if it is not too deep.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it is not advisable to bandage the wound so tightly and then treat it, as we have said, until it is healed.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The shape of the thorn-spine, from which they make a fistula, is very sharp and pointed;
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	and on the other side, not at all, because one should not bandage it as you will see below:
des emorroydes	of hemorrhoids
Emorrydes sont selonc ij. manieres: ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc,	Hemorrhoids are of two types: they can be inside the anus, like grains of resin, and they come in small and large sizes, and they ooze blood.
et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement; mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor,	There can be one or more of them, and they can be either inside or outside the anus; but those that are outside have less moisture.
et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	They ooze pus or a little watery fluid or blood, and their color is like that of the body.
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	And the treatment for those who have them inside the anus is that you instruct the patient to strain themselves until they pass the stools, and then the hemorrhoids will come out.
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	If you are in a hurry, seize it with tweezers or your fingernail, then pull out the roots.
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a .i. drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	And if the tweezers cannot hold it due to moisture, then take it with a cloth, or cotton, or a piece of cambric.
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	And pull them out with your fingers, then pluck them, and powder some hot powders on top that act as a cautery.
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, puis les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	Or you can cauterize them as it is said in the chapter on cauterization, then treat with other treatments until it is healed.
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	and if the foundations cannot come out, then cleanse the patient with a strong and harsh enema to wash away what is in the foundation, so that it can come out clearly;
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	and if the patients defecate, and if the thread comes out from the foundation, then the cure is easy;
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	and you should grab them with your fingernail or tweezers, and cut them, then treat them as we have said, until they are healthy and afraid of incision by iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere: pren .i. fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les .ij. chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille,	If you need to perform suturing in this way: take a twisted thread and insert it into a needle, then pull the thread through the top and push the needle through from the other side, and then bring both ends of the thread under the needle,
et si soit dou large; et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse .i. por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	and if it is swollen and tender; then tightly wind the thread, knot the thread, withdraw the needle, and do likewise with all the others, and leave one to drain the excess blood;
puis met sus le fondement .i. drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	then place on the wound a damp cloth soaked in rose oil or cerate, and apply it to the wound, and instruct the patient to rest;
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then leave them until they fall off, and when they have fallen off, treat the wound with ointment and other remedies until it is healed.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	from dryness of the vagina or anus
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Many times there is dryness of the bowels in the intestines, and through constriction of nature, and when the disease is old and medicine does not help.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	If you should cut with a spatulum or your nail through the skin above it, so that moisture does not reach it.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	Then dry it as much as necessary;
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	and if he cannot dry up, then start the scraping again stronger than before, until it heals and is scraped off;
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat it until it heals.
dou fremit	where it trembles
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	Antors is a small appearance that arises under the body and goes deep inside.
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	And sometimes the antors cause trembling, and it can be felt throughout the body, more so in the hands than anywhere else.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the cure is that you take a feather of a goose's quill, or a strong vulture's feather, and place this feather on the vein, so that the purple circle encompasses the vein all around.
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	Then turn your hand along the entire feather, so that you press all around the vein, and insert it deeply, and squeeze the vein from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you see fit to make this instrument of a feather of iron or steel according to this shape, and have it finely polished beneath and drawn above.
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	do not pierce it, so that it can be held in the hand and pressed firmly. And if you see fit to cauterize the vein, as described earlier in this chapter on cautery.
de la forme dou clistere	of the form of the enema
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet; et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	Sometimes an enema is made of silver or bronze, or melted copper or brass; and sometimes these instruments are small and large, depending on who they are administered to.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Those that are administered to children and the weak and painful are small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The form of the enema, whether small or large, is inserted widely into the stomach, according to this method:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez; et ait a l’un des costez .ij. pertus, et en l’autre .i.;	and he has a rupture where the abdomen is tied, as you see, and the buttocks are pierced inside; and he has two holes on one side, and one on the other;
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus,	and the abdomen where one puts the medicines of a beast's bladder or parchment, and it is pierced all around with small holes;
et ait entre chescun pertus .i. doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus .i. fil fort de fil crut tort en .x. ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	and has between each hole a distance of one finger's width, then inserts into these holes one strong thread of twisted thread in ten or so places around, and gathers the belly together like a goat;
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize; et c’est li forme dou cercle:	and when the medicine is inside, he ties it to the instrument in front with a strong thread, then clysters; and this is the shape of the circle:
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	And let the medicine not be too hot or too cold, and anoint the head of the syringe with oil or egg white, or similar thing, then insert it gently;
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses .ij. mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit,	then the minister squeezes it with both hands together, until it is empty, then withdraw the syringe and let the patient rest his legs against something,
et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet; et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	and if the medicine wants to come out, let him strain as much as he can; and if he sleeps for a night afterwards, it is all the more helpful.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you syringe him for a disorder of the stomach, and the medicine rushes out, then he should do it again until he is cured.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por .i. enfant;	And if the hemorrhoids are in the fundament or an abscess, let the enema be as fine as for a child.
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	and this is the form of the subtle enema above which the skin is stretched:
des plaies	of wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies; or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	We have already discussed in the division of the treatment of wounds; now we will discuss the treatments by hand and medicine, according to their completion.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are diverse according to how they are made, and according to the places where the wounds are made, and according to what makes them.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	The things by which wounds are made are by the impact of a stone, and cutting with a sword or knife, or spear or staff, or arrow, or similar objects.
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	Or according to the places in the body where they are made, such as a wound on the neck, or head, or leg, or belly, or liver, and similar organs;
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	And I will tell you the cure for each wound, and I will begin with simple wounds of the head, for the memory will come in its chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans,	I say that when a simple wound comes to the head, and the bone is not broken, then take care if it is from a stone or similar object, and the skin is still broken and the wound is large,
et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut: si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	and you suspect a hot abscess easily: then have the patient bleed from the head immediately if there is little blood coming from the wound, and let the bleeding be in the opposite direction to the injured part;
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	and let the patient avoid surfeit of wine and rich foods.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	And if he will not bleed, then his diet should be reduced, and he should drink no wine nor eat no meat;
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	and put sorrel on the wound, if a hot abscess develops, wet cotton in rose oil only, or in astringent wine;
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	and if there is no hot abscess, put sorrel on the wound if it has all its blood and has not been moved by the wind; I will describe the powder in a little while.
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and if it has been moved by the air, put it on some ointments until it is healed.
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	And if the wound is large, like that of a sword, and the lips cannot be brought together with tenting, then bring them together by suturing, as I will describe for abdominal wounds.
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope; puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir,	If the wound is exposed to the bone, and it can be picked at, and only holds on by a bit, then cut it away; then cure the wound with medicine, and restore hard flesh in place of skin,
et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	and instruct the patient to eat coarse foods, such as testicles and cooked wheat, as well as meat, and similar things.
Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure;	And if you find suppuration in the skin, and it is not near the bone, then cut away the suppuration completely, and then cure it;
et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	and if there is an artery in the wound or vein, which does not clot, and cannot be staunched with medicine, then cut the artery, and if you find it dislocated, then tie it with a thread;
et se ceu ne profite mie, si la cauterize.	and if this does not help, then cauterize it.
Et se ces plaies sont petites et simples, si est li cure legiere: et est que tu mettes ens ceste poudre qui soude ainsois que li ars l’ait muee.	And if these wounds are small and simple, the cure is easy; you must apply this powder that will heal as soon as it has burned.
Et li maniere de la poudre si est: pren encens une partie; sanc de dragon .ij. parties; chalz vive .iij. parties, et le poudre subtilment,	And the method of making the powder is this: take incense one part, dragon's blood two parts, quicklime three parts, and grind them together finely.
et emple la plaie, et l’estraint forment, tant qu’elle s’aerse bien et se joigne a tout son sanc;	and apply it to the wound, pressing firmly until it scabs over and joins with the rest of the skin.
et puis la lie bien, et la laisse sens desliier, s’elle n’enfle; car on n’oste la madicine tant qu’ele soit sanee.	and then bind it well, and leave it untied if it does not swell; for the medicine is not removed until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on ceu de chalz soulement, quant on n’ait l’encens ne lou sanc de dragon, mais que li ars n’ait muee la plaie.	And sometimes one does this with chalk alone, when one doesn't have incense or dragon's blood, but that the wound is moved by the fire.
Et se li ars ait mueit la plaie, meismement en esteit, si n’i met om mie ceste poudre;	And if the fire has moved the wound, it should be treated in the same way, and no powder should be applied.
mais met sus aucuns oignemens digestis, ou poulz de farine d’orge faites d’aigue et de miel, tant qu’ele giete bowe;	but one should place upon it some digestive ointments, or a poultice made of barley flour with water and honey, until the swelling goes down.
puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then treat other wounds until he is healed.
Et se li brisure d’os vient avec la plaie, et elle est petite, si l’estrai as pinceures subtilz;	And if the fracture of the bone comes with the wound and it is small, I will extract it with fine pincers;
et je vos dirai ci aprés les brisures dou chief.	and then I will tell you about head fractures.
de la plaie dou col	about the wound on the neck
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	If the wound is on the neck and it is simple, there is no difference between it and that of the head, but if the nerves of the neck or the artery are cut.
Se c’est li ners, si n’i a autre engien que laissier la cure, et n’i mettre nulle chose restraignant, car il nuit as ners et les fait retraire;	If it is the nerve, there is no other treatment but to leave it alone and not apply anything constricting, for it harms the nerves and makes them retreat.
et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres;	And do not apply anything cold to the wound, for the substance of the nerves is cold, and their continuation is with the brain, which is the highest member.
mais soit li medicine souez, si com chalz lavee en aigue douce, et mellee avec oile roset, et cucie lavee ausi en aigue douce,	But let there be medicine beneath, such as cold wash in lukewarm water, and mixed with rose oil, and cucumber washed also in lukewarm water,
et autres pieres de mine selonc ceste maniere, et oignemens moistes.	and other moist stones according to this method.
Et se li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound is large, cut and bind it, then heal it.
Et se les plaies sont parfondes et ele est chevee et pleinne de bowe, si la perce ou plus bas leu;	And if the wounds are deep and she is pregnant and full of bowels, then pierce her in a lower place.
et se li artere est copee, et decorremens de sanc en vient, si la desoivre, et la loie, et la cauterize se mestier est;	and if the artery is cut and bleeding ensues, then tie it off, and ligate it, and cauterize it if necessary.
et se li espinee de la gorge est copee, ou li keurs, et li conduiz est gardez, par coi la viande va,	and if the spine of the throat is cut, or the bones, and the windpipe is kept safe, through which the food passes,
si cout le keur sus la cainne de la gorge, et ne touchier la gorge mais la remet selonc sa figure naturel;	if he cuts the bone on the side of the throat, and doesn't touch the throat but puts it back in its natural position;
et puis l’estrain avenanment, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le cure d’oignemens desechans tant qu’il soit sanez;	and then he stretches it gently, and leaves it for a few days, then he treats it with cleansing ointments until it is healed;
et se li plaie a fait empression en l’os, si la quier;	and if the wound has made an impression in the bone, then he should;
et s’il i a pieces d’os, si les trai fuers toz se tu pues, et ces que tu ne pues avoir, si laisse tant que li plaie porrisse,	and if there are bone fragments, pull out all those you can, and leave those you cannot reach until the wound heals.
et soit desevree et aligie li issue;	and the dislocation should be made smooth and aligned;
et se li plaie est fresche, si poudre sus la poudre que j’ai dit.	and if the wound is fresh, apply the powder I described earlier.
Et s’il a en la plaie os et il i a fistule, si la cure ensi com j’ai dit en son chapistre.	And if there is bone in the wound and it has a fistula, treat it as I described in its chapter.
de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	of a wound from a spear or knife
Se c’est cop de lance ou de coutel, et li plaie est parfonde, si regarde se de la plaie saut ventositez cant li malaides alainne: saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	If it is a spear or knife wound, and the wound is deep, then observe whether the wound breathes winds: know therefore that the wound is mortal;
et s’elle n’est parfonde, et elle est fresche a tout son sanc, si n’i mettre mie a la premiere houre la poudre, ne ne la liier mie por le sanc que ne demorse em parfont,	and if it is not deep, and it is fresh with all its blood, then do not put the powder on it at first, nor bind it because of the blood that comes out profusely,
et reviegne au cuer, et ocie lou malaide;	and returns to the heart, and heals the patient;
mais i met oignement atractif, et le lie .ij. fois le jor;	but I apply an attractive ointment, and bind it .ii. times a day;
et se tu n’as oignement, si met en la plaie viel coton por succier fuers la moistor,	and if you do not have ointment, put old cotton in the wound to draw out moisture,
et fai dormir le malaide sus la plaie .iij. jors, ou .iiij., ou plusors;	and let the patient sleep on the wound for .iii. days, or .iv., or more;
si n’i venra mie spasme, ne tremor male de cuer n’es traingnemens d’alainne;	if a spasm or tremor of the heart does not come, nor shudders of the soul, nor twitches of the eyes;
et quant tu vois les bones dispositions, si saiches que li plaie est sauve.	and when you see the bones aligned, then you know the wound is healed.
Cure la donques de tentes et d’autres cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Heal it therefore with poultices and other remedies until it is healed;
et s’elle ne puet saner, et oevre, adés saiches que il i a fistule; si la cure si com on doit.	and if it cannot heal, and there is pus, then you know there is a fistula; then treat it as one should.
Et se li plaie est d’incision d’espee ou de coutel, et elle est simple, ou pis ou au dos, si la cure de ceu qui est devant;	And if the wound is from a cut by a sword or knife, and it is superficial, on the face or the back, then treat it as one should;
s’elle est grans, de cousture; et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	if it is large, then stitch it up; and if it is small, then use powder on it; and if it has gone deep into the bone and has broken off fragments, then clean the wound and draw out any foreign objects if they are loose;
et s’il ne sont desevrez, si laisse porrir la plaie, si aligera li estractions;	and if they are not loose, then let the wound fester until you can extract them easily;
et des autres plaies as autres membres est li jugemens si com nos avons dit.	and for other wounds in other parts of the body, make your judgment as we have said.
dou derrompement dou ventre	a hernia
Li derompemens dou ventre est grans et moiens et petis;	There are great, medium, and small ruptures of the belly;
de la grant plaie saut aucune fois li intestine, ou li ners des intestines, par coi li intromission d’aus;	from the large wound sometimes the intestine, or the nerve of the intestines, by which the entry of air;
et li costure est plus malaisie, et aucune fois vaut pis li petite plaie que li grans,	and the sewing is more difficult, and sometimes the smaller wound is worse than the larger,
por ceu c’on remet plus a poinnes les intestines en, s’on ne les i remet de chaut en chaut;	because one puts the intestines back in more easily, if one does not put them in warm and cold;
por ce que li intestine enflent tantost qu’il sentent le froit, si rentrent plus a poinnes,	because the intestines swell as soon as they feel cold, they contract more with pins,
et por ceu vaut mues li moieinne plaie, por ceu c’on ramoine mues l’intestine a son leu que as autres .ij.	and for this reason the female wound is better, for this reason one resets the intestine in its place more .ij.
Et saiches que li routure dou ventre est selonc .iiij. manieres:	And know that there are .iiij ways of rupture in the belly:
les .ij. costures communes avienent en la costure dou ventre,	the .ij common sutures occur in the suture of the abdomen,
et li costure des autres plaies dou cors et .ij. autres costures propres sont communes as autres plaies;	and the stitches of other wounds on the body, and two other special stitches, are common to all other wounds;
et toutevoie elles sont plus propres avec la costure dou ventre, et je dirai une chescune et declairerai.	yet they are most suitable for stomach wounds, and I will describe each one and explain them:
Je di que quant li plaie est petite, et aucune chose de l’intestine ist fuer,	I say that when the wound is small, and some part of the intestine has come out,
et griés chose est dou remettre, ceu est par l’une des .ij. manieres:	and if it is difficult to put back inside, this can be done by one of two methods:The following text is a medieval medical treatise written in Old French, around the 12th-13th centuries.
ou por la petitece de la plaie, si com nos avons dit,	or for the smallness of the wound, as we have said,
ou por ce que li intestine est enflez por le froit.	or because the intestines are swollen due to cold.
Et quant il est frois, eschaufez lou en teil maniere:	And when it is cold, warm it in this way:
moillie une esponge ou .i. mol drapeil en aigue tede soulement,	wet a sponge or soft cloth with tepid water only,
ou tu cuis en aigue squinant et cipre et spique,	or you cook in water squinant and cypress and spike,
et arose l’intestine tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	and the intestines until the swelling is removed;
et aucune fois fait ce vins restraingnans, et est muedre que awe soule por desenfler.	and sometimes makes this restraining wine, and it is mixed with water to reduce swelling.
Et quant tu vois l’enfleure departir, si amoiste l’intestine d’aigue ou altee et malves soient cuites,	And when you see the swelling leaving, then mix the intestines with water or altée and maliciousness be cooked,
car par ceu est aligie li entree a poc de chose;	because it restricts the entrance to a small amount;
et s’il n’i puet entrer, si fent un poc la plaie a l’estrument de coi on cope les emorroydes;	and if it cannot enter, they make a small wound with an instrument that is used to cut out hemorrhoids;
et li premiere cure est muedre que li taille,	and the first treatment is bloodletting rather than cutting,
que nus n’i doit taillier sens grant necessiteit n’i ait;	that one shouldn't cut unless there is a great need;
et c’est li estrumens por le fendre:	and this is the instrument to split it with:
si trenche dedens en la corbeure et defuer non, et vez ci la forme:	if you cut inside the curve and not out, and see here the shape:
Et quant li plaie est enlargie, et li intestine saut fuer,	And when the wound is enlarged and the intestines jump out,
si le remet arer selonc la forme naturel en son leu propre,	if you put it back according to its natural shape in its proper place,
se tu en as pooir, car ce vaut mues.	if you have the power, for this is worth it.
Quant li plaie est large, et elle est en la partie desoz lou ventre,	When the wound is large and it is in the lower part of the belly,
si covient que tu faices gesir lou malaide sus son dos,	you should make the patient lie on his back,
et met ses jambes plus haut que son chief;	and put his legs higher than his head;
et s’elle est en la partie desoz le ventre,	and if it is in the area below the belly,
si met le chief et le pis plus haut que les parties desoz,	put the head and foot higher than the parts below,
et ausi se li routure dou ventre est en l’une des .ij. parties	and also if the rupture of the belly is in one of the two parts
si met t’entente en ceu que li partie navree soit plus haute que li autre;	put the affected part higher than the other;
et ensi covient amenistrer ceu que je dis en plaies grans et moienes.	and so you must apply what I say to large and medium wounds.
Es plaies petites met ceu que t’est apparilliet,	For small wounds, use whatever is available to you:
puis aies entre tes mains .i. ministre pitous ki teigne toute la routure a sa main,	then have ready in your hands a minister of pity who will press the wound all around with his hand,
et assemble les levres;	and gather the lips;
et c’est la maniere commune de costures,	and this is the common method of sewing,
et est que tu preignes une aguille ou plusors, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce de la plaie,	take a needle or several, depending on the width of the wound,
puis laisse des le chief de la plaie .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une aguille ou il ait .i. boin fil fort;	then leave about an inch of space from the head of the wound, and pierce with a needle where there is a good strong thread;
et perce les .ij. chiés dou cuir avec les .ij. chiés dou siphac,	and pierce the two pieces of skin with the two pieces of thread,
qui est desoz le cuir dedens, tant que tu la faices percier de celle partie,	which is under the skin inside, as far as you make it pierce from that part,
et assemble les .ij. chief dou siphac les .iiij. ensamble;	and brings together the two heads of the vein, and then the four come together;
puis l’estrain d’un fil double entor l’aguille de .ij. pars,	then draw it with a double thread around the needle in two parts,
puis assemble les .ij. chiés de la plaie avenanment,	then bring together the two heads of the wound properly,The following text is a medieval medical treatise written in Old French, around the 12th-13th centuries.
et puis laisse .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une autre aguille;	and then leave.i. space, and I push another needle through;
puis la lie dou fil si com tu as fait la premiere aguille,	then tie the thread as you did with the first needle,
et ne cesser de ceu faire selonc ceu que tu as mestier des aguilles,	and do not stop doing this according to what you need in terms of needles,
tant que toute li plaie soit restrainte;	until the entire wound is closed;
et soient les aguilles moienes, entre subtilz et grosses,	and let the needles be medium-sized, between fine and thick,
car les aguilles subtilz copent toute la char, et les trop grosses si ne pueent mie bien entrer:	because fine needles pierce all the flesh, and too thick ones cannot pierce well:
por ceu covient qu’elles soient moienes;	therefore they should be medium-sized;
et ne covient mie bouter les aguilles trop au defuer de la char et dou cuir,	and one must not push the needles too deep into the flesh and through the skin,
k’elles ne copent et oevrent la plaie devant la soudure;	that they do not close and open the wound before the solder;
et puis cope les chiés des aguilles, qu’elles ne blecent lou malaide au dormir,	and then cover the heads of the needles, so that they do not hurt the patient while sleeping,
et i met tentes ou drapelz au chiés des aguilles por mues tenir,	and put tents or pieces of cloth on the needle heads to keep them in place,
et les laisse tant que li plaie soit soudee;	and leave them until the wound is sealed;
et ceste maniere de costure as aguilles est plus covenauble en petites plaies,	and this method of sewing with needles is more suitable for small wounds,
car il i soffist une aguille ou .ij.	because you only need one needle or two.
Li seconde costure si est commune,	The second stitch is common,
et est que tu assemble les .ij. chiés dou cuir et les .ij. chiés dou syfac ensamble a une aguille ou il ait .i. fort fil moien;	and it is that you join the two pieces of skin and the two pieces of the wound together with one needle, or a strong thin thread;
et quant tu avras perciez ces chiez toz .iiij. ensamble,	and when you have pierced all four together,
si ramoinne l’aguille a la partie ou tu as encomenciet, en la maniere c’on cout les dras;	then bring the needle back to the part where you started, in the manner that one sews cloth;
et met d’espaice entre chescune costure la grossece d’un menor doi;	and space each stitch apart by the thickness of a thumb;
ceste costure sevent li home,	this stitch should be seven times the length of the needle;
et je cousi une plaie c’uns hons avoit ou ventre,	and I sewed up a wound that a man had on his belly,
qui estoit navrez d’un coutel,	which had been made by a knife,
et estoit li plaie plus d’une palme de grant,	and the wound was more than a palm-width wide,
et issoit des intestines bien .ij. palmes de grant,	and the intestines protruded well over .10. palms wide,
et estoit li plaie enmi le ventre.	and the wound was in his belly.
Je li ramenai l’intestine puis k’il ot esteit .xxiiij. houres fuer,	I returned the intestine to where it had been 24 hours prior
et fut li plaie soudee jusc’a .xv. jors, et le curai, et fut sanez.	and the wound was sewn up for 15 days, and I treated it, and it healed.
Et li mire l’avoient jugiet qu’il morroit, et ce fut miracle;	And they had judged that he would die, and this was a miracle;
et ne le curai mie d’oignement, car je estoie en .i. leu ou on n’en trovoit point, ne nule medicines;	and I did not treat it with ointment because I was in a place where no such things could be found, neither medicine nor anything else;
et metoie sens plus sus la plaie coton viel .ij. fois le jor, et le lavoie d’aigue de miel tant qu’il fut sanez.	and I applied cotton wool soaked in honey to the wound twice a day, and washed it with honeyed water until it healed.
Or vos dirai les .ij. propres manieres de cousture:	Now I will tell you two proper methods of suturing:
pren l’aguille, et la boute des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens;	take the needle and insert it from the outside just into the inside;
quant elle a perciet le keur de droit en droit, si lai le chief dou siphac ou cousteit ou tu as bouteit l’aguille,	when it has pierced the heart directly, then insert the needle into the vein or artery where you are going to inject.
et la fai percier d’autre part des la partie dedens jusc’a celi defuer;	and let it pierce through from another part of the body into the chest cavity;
et li entendemens de ceste costure si est que tu cous ausi com li peletier font les pelz,	and the understanding of this suturing is that you sew as the leather workers do to hides,
et que tu laisses une fois le syfac d’une part, et le reprent d’autre, tant que li costure soit toute acomplie.	and that you leave one side of the vein open, and close the other, so that the suturing is complete.
Li seconde maniere de costure, que Galiens dist proprement,	The second manner of sewing, which Galen calls properly,
si est si com aucun font, qui assemblent les .ij. parties ensamble naturelment,	if it is as when two parts are joined together naturally,
et apploient l’un des chief dou syfac a l’autre chief, en teil maniere:	and they apply one end to the other end, in such a way:
fiche une aguille ou chief dou mirach prochiene, et fai percier celui leu soulement,	stick an needle or awl close to the edge, and only pierce that spot,
et laisse les .ij. chiés dou syfac;	and leave the two shoulders of the syringe;
puis torne l’aguille, et la fai percier des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens,	then turn the needle and pierce it from the outside inwards, through to the inside,
as .ij. chiés dou syfac;	as the two shoulders of the syringe;
puis fai percier l’un et l’autre des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, en .ij. autres chiés dou mirach que sont on l’autre costeit;	then pierce one and the other from the outside inwards, through to the inside, in two other shoulders of the syringe that are on the other side;
et c’est li muedre maniere de costure et li plus commune.	and this is the principal method of sewing and the most common one.
Galiens si dist ceste parolle, et aucun le tesmoignent,	Galen says these words, and some testify to it,
c’on doit coudre le ventre a .ij. aguilles, ou il ait fil en chescune;	that one should sew the belly with two needles, having thread in each;
et doit on bouter l’une aguille d’une part, et l’autre d’autre, en la maniere de ces qui cousent corroies;	and one must push one needle from one side and the other from the other, in the manner of those who sew hide;
et saiches que quant li routure est enmi lou ventre,	and know that when the hernia is in the belly,
si est li cousture plus griez que des autres leus dou ventre.	the sutures are more difficult than in other places in the belly.
Li jugemens de la plaie si est telz com li jugemens des autres plaies:	The judgment of the wound is such as the judgment of other wounds:
et est que quant tu trueves la plaie fresche a tout son sanc, ainsois que li ars l’ait muee,	and it is that when you find the fresh wound full of blood, as long as the heat has not moved it,
si remet arer l’intestine, et lou cout; puis met sus la poudre enjanrant char,	if one re-inserts the intestine, and sews it up; then place the cauterizing powder on a piece of cloth,
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucun oignement que soit present, tant que li plaie bowe;	and if he burns it, he should immediately apply some ointment to cool the wound;
et chicent li fil, et soient soudez li sifac, et li mirach;	and they cut the thread, and sew up the anus, and the navel;
puis cure la plaie si com les autres, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then clean the wound as with the others, until it is healed;
et se tu n’as medicines, si met sus, tantost qu’ele comance a giter bowe, coton viel,	and if you do not have medicine, place old cotton wool on it as soon as it starts to ooze pus
et le remue .ij. fois le jor tant k’il soit sanez.	and move it 14 times a day until it heals.
Car tu n’as mestier d’autre medicine en plusors dispositions cant les plaies sont simples;	For you do not need any other medicine for various wounds that are simple;
et se tu doutes que li plaie ne faice communiteit as membres principelz,	and if you doubt that the wound is causing infection in the principal members,
si covient ke tu moilles lainne legiere en oile de tempree chalor, ou en oile roset,	if you should moisten a light woolen cloth in tempered oil, or in rose oil,
et la met entor les angres, et desoz les asselles;	and place it around the angles, and under the armpits;
et s’il sent dolor ou porriture en bouelz, et maintes fois avient,	and if there is pain or swelling in the bowels, and this happens many times,
si les clisterize de vin noir tede, et meismement se li porriture vient jusc’a l’intestine;	then let him take enemas of warm red wine, especially if the swelling comes up to the intestines;
et le perce dedens, et saiches que quant c’est li gros intestines, si est plus legier a saner que li petis.	and pierces inside it, and know that when it is the large intestine, it is easier to heal than the small one.
Li intestine qui est apelez «jeun» ne puet saner quant il est navrez,	The intestine which is called "young" cannot heal when it is raw,
et c’est por la planteit des voinnes que i sont, et por la subtiliteit de tout le cors, et l’aprochement de sa nature des ners.	and it is because of the thinness of the veins that they are, and because of the subtlety of the whole body, and the closeness of its nature to the nerves.
Et si li zirbe saut de la plaie, si le remet arrier ausi com l’intestine, tandis qu’il est fres;	And if the thread jumps out of the wound, it puts it back as far as the intestine, while it is fresh;
et s’il est vielz et devenus vers ou noir, si covient que tu lies le leu qui est noir, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne,	and if it is old and turned white or black, you should tie the area that is black so that no blood flow comes from it,
car il i a voinnes et arteres;	because there are veins and arteries;
puis cope ceu qui est entre le liien,	then cut what is between the ligature,
et met les .ij. chiés pendans des la partie desoz la plaie jusque defuer por aligier l’estraction quant li zirbes chiet, et li plaie bowe.	and place the two ends of the thread from under the wound up to the edge to ease the extraction when the thread is pulled, and the wound is closed.
de la routure dou boueil	of the boiling route
Quant li intestine est rons, et li plaie est petite,	When the intestine is torn and the wound is small,
si la puet on restorer en aucuns homes,	one can mend it in some ways,
por ceu que je vis que uns hons fut navrez ou ventre d’une lance;	because I saw a man who was pierced in the belly with a lance;
et estoit li plaie au destre de l’estomac,	was located on the right side of the stomach,
et fut envillie et devint fistule, et en issoit li egestion et li ventositez;	and became a fistula, and from it came digested food and wind;
je i mis cure selonc ceu que je poi, et ne cessai de subtilier tant qu’il fut sanez, et li leus soudez.	I applied treatment according to what I knew, and did not stop cauterizing until it healed and the wounds closed.
Et quant je le vis souder, je doutai que li malaides n’eust mal en son ventre;	And when I saw it healing, I feared that the patient had discomfort in his abdomen;
et il n’i ot point de mal, mais demora en millors dispositions, et menjans et bevans;	and it did not cause harm but persisted in better conditions, eating and drinking;
et dirent aucun experimentors que quant il a petite plaie en l’intestine, qu’il doit estre liiez en teil maniere:	And some experimenters say that when there is a small wound in the intestines, it must be bound in such a way:
pren fremis a grans testes, puis assemble les levres de la plaie,	take fine thread from a large testicle, then bring together the edges of the wound,
et quant li fremis ait overte la bouche, si la met sus les .ij. levres,	and when the thread has opened the mouth, he places it on top of the two lips,
si qu’elle estraigne sa bouche sus;	if it pulls out its mouth upward;
et puis li cope la teste, et ce se tient si qu’il ne puet desliier,	and then grips the head, and holds on so that it cannot escape,
puis met .i. autre fremit aprés en celle maniere que devant, tant que li plaie soit toute porprise;	then puts another grip after in the same way as before, until the wound is completely grasped;
et cout la plaie.	and checks the wound.
Cil chief si s’aerdent en l’intestine, et ne vient nulle nuisance au malaide,	If they are absorbed into the intestines and do not harm the patient,
et se puet on liier l’intestine d’un fil subtil qui est copez de l’intestine d’une beste,	and one can ligate the intestine with a fine thread cut from the intestine of an animal,
en teil maniere:	in such a way:
pren le chief de cest fil d’intestine que soit mout descharnez,	take the end of this intestinal thread that is very dried out,
et puis lie au chief de cest fil .i. fil de lin subtil tort,	and then tie to the head of this thread a thread of fine twisted linen;
puis boute le fil en l’aguille, et en cout l’intestine, et le ramoinne en la routure;	then push the thread through the needle, and sew up the intestine, and return it to its proper place;
et ceste maniere de costure de fremis nen est fuers que selonc la voie de fiance et d’esperance;	and this method of stitching a hernia is not without risk, according to the way of faith and hope;
et se li plaie est grans et large, meismement quant elle est en l’un des grailes intestines, si n’i a engien ne santeit, fuer que subtiliteit.	and if the wound is large and wide, especially when it is in one of the small intestines, there is no healing or health, unless with great subtlety.
de fistule ou qu’ele soit	of fistula wherever it may be
Saiches que toute plaie ou aposteme, quant il enveillist, si est apelee universement «fistule»,	You should know that any wound or abscess, when it wakes up, is universally called a "fistula."
et meismement quant elle est chevee et rent bowe.	And especially when it is deep and narrow.
Et fistule est selonc la verteit nodation fautree dure et blainche, ou on ne sent dolor,	A fistula is a hard white swelling without pain,
et est ausi chevee com li penne d’un oiseil;	and it has a head like the beak of a bird;
et aucune fois en saut clere bowe, et autre fois espesse;	sometimes it jumps very high, and sometimes low to the ground.
aucune fois poc, et autre fois assez;	sometimes it poops, and sometimes not much;
et je en ai jai parleit en la division des plaies, que toute plaie que n’est sanee, et il n’i a char,	and I have spoken about this in the section on wounds, that any wound that is not healed and there is no discharge,
ce n’est fuers que par une des .viiij. causes:	It is caused by one of eight reasons:
c’est a savoir, par la petitece dou sanc ou cors;	namely, by the smallness of blood or body;
ou por sa malice;	or because of its wickedness;
ou por ceu qu’il i a char dure dedens, et sus les levres, que n’i laisse naistre char;	or because there is hard flesh within, and on the lips, that does not allow flesh to grow;
ou il i a trop de bowe;	where there is too much bowing;
ou li leus est porris, et li matiere est de male qualiteit;	or the skin is perished, and the matter is of poor quality;
ou li medicine n’est mie bone en la cure;	or the medicine is not good for the treatment;
ou por ceu que li corruption est maniere de pestilence;	or because the corruption is of a pestilential nature;
ou por la proprieteit en la region est tardive li digestion, et tarde li santeit, et enflee par nature;	Or by virtue of the nature of the region digestion is tardy, and health delayed, and it swells by nature.
ou il i a voinnes ou os:	Or there are veins or bones:
et j’ai ja mostreit toutes ces causes, et les signes, et les cures de medicines en la division.	And I have already shown all these causes, and the signs, and the cures of medicine in the division.
Or covient que je te faice a savoir la cure de fistule qui est faite par oevre de mains.	Now I must tell you about the treatment of a fistula that is done by hand.
Saiches que fistule avient en tous membres dou cors;	Know that a fistula occurs in all parts of the body;
car il i a fistules que vienent as grans voines, et as arteres, et as ners,	for there are fistulas that come from large veins and arteries and nerves,
ou au syfac, ou a l’intestine, ou a la vessie, ou a aucunes des costes,	or the face, or intestines, or bladder, or any of the sides,
ou a l’espinee dou dos, ou a aucune jointe des mains ou des piez;	or to the ears, head, eyes, limbs, and teeth.
et si a teil que vient a la proprieteit dou membre principeil, et as semblans leus.	and if it affects the principal member itself, and similar areas.
Et toutes les fistules que sont de ceste maniere sont de grief sanation, et n’i a fors que labour, et ignorance;	And all the fistulas that are in this way are of great harm, and there is nothing but labor and ignorance;
et se il i a aucune fistule que ne veigne mie jusc’a leu que j’ai dit, et tu as fiance de la cure,	and if there is any fistula that does not come to the place I have described, and you are confident in the treatment,
et tu la vues conoistre, si pren une tente d’arain ou de fer, se li fistule est droite, si la quier;	and you see it, take a tent of iron or steel, if the fistula is straight, so take it;
et se li fistule est torte, si la cerche d’une subtil tente de plonc,	and if the fistula is crooked, then probe with a thin, blunt instrument,
car li plons se ploie mues entor la tortuositeit;	because the blunt instrument will bend around the crook;
et se li fistule a mains pertus et tu ne la pues mie bien cerchier par tentes,	and if the fistula has a narrow opening and you cannot probe it well with instruments,
si la clisterize par l’un des pertus,	if you cleanse it through one of the openings,
car la moistors si cort d’un pertus a autre, et la mundifie;	for moisture quickly travels from one hole to another and cleanses.
puis la quier saigement a ton pooir, que tu conoisses s’il i a os ou nerf, et est chevee em parfont,	then you should let it bleed until you can tell if there is bone or nerve involved, and if it is deeply embedded.
et demande bien au malaide de la dolor qu’il sent au presser de ta main, et le leu ou il la sent;	and ask the patient about the pain they feel when you press with your hand, and where they feel it.
et quant tu savras vraiement le leu ou elle est, et s’elle est loing de jointure, ou de nerf, ou d’artere ou de voine,	and when you know the exact location, if it is far from a joint, nerve, artery or vein,
ou en aucuns des leus que je t’ai dit, si la cope selonc ceu que je t’ai dit,	or in any of the ways I have told you, if the wound according to what I have said;
et oste fuer la fautreure et les chars corrumpues que sont dedens;	and remove the foulness and corrupted flesh within;
et puis la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee,	and then treat the wound until it is healed;
et se li fistule est bien parfonde de droit endroit, si covient que tu copes em parfont, tant com tu pues,	and if the fistula is very deep in a straight line, you must cut it open as much as you can,
puis i met tentes moillies en medicine ague, et les boute jusc’au chief de la fistule,	then I wet tents in medicine ague, and I press them to the head of the fistula
tant que li medicine corrode la superfluiteit qui est demoree au fons;	until the medicine corrodes the excess that remains at the bottom
et puis i met oignemens enjanrans sainne char, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and then I apply ointments to heal the wound, until it is healed
et s’il n’est sanez par ceu, si le cauterize si com nos avons dit,	and if it is not healed by this method, then cauterize it as we have said,
et se li os est corrompus de la fistule, si le cope.	and if the bone is corrupted by the fistula, then cut it off.
Se voinne ou ners ne te greve ou membres principelz, si com nos avons dit;	If a vein or nerve causes you distress in your limbs, as we have said;
et se li os est descovers, et il i a corruption et noiror, si lou reis tant que li corruption soit toute ostee,	and if the bone is exposed and there is corruption and darkness, then cut it until all the corruption is removed,
puis le cure de choses enjanrans char tant qu’il soit sanez;	then cleanse it with things that are cooling until it is healed;
et s’il n’est sanez, et rent bowe si com devant,	and if it is not healthy, and return bow as before,
saiches que tu n’es mie alez jusc’a font:	know that you have not gone to the fountain;
si descuevre et quier tant que tu soies au fons,	if you uncover and desire as much as you are at the bottom,
et oste toute la corruption, puis restore le leu;	and remove all corruption, then restore the place;
et s’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	and if it is so without pain, that is good.
Se ceu non, saiches que la corruption est trop en parfont, que tu n’i pues avenir;	If not, know that the corruption is too deep for you to reach.
si n’i a autre engien que dou lassier a nature;	if there is no other way than to let nature take its course,
et s’il i a i petit os corrumput, et tu le pues traire as tenailles,	and if there is a small corrupt bone that you can pull out with tweezers,
si l’estrai a .i. estrument covenauble a ceu,	if he removes it with an instrument suitable for this purpose,
et s’il i a maint os, si les trai trestoz, ne n’en laissier nes un;	and if there are many bones, he should pull them out one by one;
et se li moistor te fait contraire, et il n’i a error ne paour,	and if the moisture makes it difficult, and there is no error or fear,
si cope et moistor et char, et delivre les os.	then cut through flesh and moisture and free the bones.
Et se tu ne les pues oster a une houre, si met sus la plaie chose enjanrant porriture,	And if you cannot remove them in one hour, place something on the wound to prevent putrefaction,
et laisse tant que li leus soit porris entor les os,	and let it remain until the pus has collected around the bone,
et adonc si avront plus legierement les os;	and then they will have the bones more easily;
et se c’est uns grans os, si com de jambe ou de cuisse,	and if it is a large bone, such as of the leg or thigh,
si reis tant soulement la corruption tant que li noiror soit toute ostee,	if you only treat the corruption until the darkness is completely removed,
puis restoure la plaie;	then restore the wound;
et s’il en i a grant partie dou corrumput, et vient jusc’a mole de l’os;	and if there is a large amount of corruption and it reaches to the bone;
si le covient soier et coper tout jusc’a la corruption, et puis le cure tant qu’il soit soudez;	if you should cut away and cover everything until the corruption is reached, and then treat it until it is healed;
et je te dirai d’une fistule qui avint .i. home en sa jambe,	and I will tell you about a fistula that happened to a man on his leg,
si que tu i preignes exemple et aide en ton ovraige.	so that you can take example and help in your work.
Il fut .i. jovencelz entor .xxx. ans, qui ot une dolor en sa jambe d’une cause que vint dedens le cors,	He was a young man of about thirty years old who had pain in his leg for a cause that came from within the body,
tant que les matieres vinrent a la jambe, et fut enflee d’un gros aposteme, et n’ot point de cause defuer por ovrir;	and he could not lift his foot or leg. So the matter came to the leg and it was swollen with a large abscess, and there was no reason to open it;
mais li mire par lor folie ovrerent tant sus que li apostemes ovri,	but through their madness they worked so much that the abscesses opened,
et en corroient mout de matieres, et devint fistule, et i vint mout de pertus que tuit gitoient bowe et moistor dou cors;	and many matters flowed out and became a fistula, and there came many openings which all discharged pus and moisture from the body;
et maint mire i mirent cure entor .ij. ans, et n’i ot nul saige en l’art de mains,	and many of them had treatment for two years, and there was no wise man in the art of medicine,
tant que je i fui apelez, et vi sa jambe et les medicines dont on le curoit,	until I was called to him, and I saw his leg and the medicines with which he was being treated,
et ceu que corroit par les pertus a grant cors;	and what ran through the holes in the body
et devenoit rouges li cors dou jouvenceil, et avoit color citrine.	and became red with the juice of the young vine, and had a citron colour.
Je boutai une tente en l’un de ces pertus, et puis cerchai toz les pertus,	I pitched a tent at one of these holes, and then blocked up all the holes,
et trovai que li uns venoit encontre l’autre de toutes les parties de la jambe.	and found that they came into contact with each other from all sides of the leg.
Je me hastai donques, et copai en l’un des pertus tant que je descovri une partie de l’os,	I hurried therefore, and struck one of the openings so hard that I uncovered a part of the bone,
et le trovai corrumput et perciet, et venoit li corruption jusc’a l’os dedens;	and found it rotten and pierced all the way to the bone inside;
je soiai ceu qui m’aparissoit de l’os corrumput, et cuidai qu’il n’i eust autre corruption, fuer que celi que je ostai;	I removed what appeared to be rotten bone, and believed that there was no other corruption except for that which I had taken out;
et comensai a restourer la plaie de medicines sodans par lonc tens, et ne pot souder;	and began to heal the wound with strong medicines for a long time, but it would not heal;
et puis rencomensai, et descovri l’os si com devant,	and then recommenced, and exposed the bone as before,
et trovai la corruption continuee en l’os, et la soiai, et puis l’ostai, et me penai de souder le leu;	and found the corruption continuing in the bone, and I cut it out, and then removed it, and worked to soud the place;
mais je ne pou tant que je copai entor une palme de l’os, et le traï fuer a tout son mole,	but I could not until I had split the bone for almost a palm's width, and drove it out from all around its socket,
puis le restourai de medicines; et il fut sanez et soudez hastanment,	then restored it with remedies; and it was healed and souded firmly,
et ne covint plus rencomencier l’ovraige fors por la foibleté dou malaide, qui ne pooit soffrir,	and one must not repeat the procedure except for the weakness of the patient, who cannot endure it,
et por la paour de mort que je avoie de lui.	and for fear of his death that I had for him.
Car por l’evacuation sanglotoit sovent, mais il fut sanez entierement,	For often due to bloodletting he bled profusely, yet he was completely healed,
et nasquit en leu de l’os une char dure, et fut de bone disposition et n’ot point de nuisement ne de contraire dou tout en tout, ne a l’aleir ne a venir.	and in the place of the bone a hard lump formed, and he was in good health with no harm or ill-effect anywhere, nor any difficulty in walking or moving.
Et se li os est brisiez en aucun leu dou cors, si le covient soier en ceste maniere:	And if the bone is broken in any part of the body, it must be bound up in this way:
pren .i. liien, et l’estrain au chief de l’os qui apert,	take a cord and wind it around the head of the bone which is open,
et comande aucun k’il l’estende en haut;	and have someone pull it upward;
et met .i. autre lien de lainne plus gros dou premier liien, et le lie sus la char qui est desor l’os,	and take another cord of thicker linen than the first one and tie it over the flesh that is above the bone,
et estent le chief, si que tu traies la char corrumpue au desoz,	and are the head, so that you draw out the corrupted flesh from below,
et descuevre la char sus le leu ou tu vues soier, que li soie ne blece la char;	and expose the flesh above the area where you see swelling, so that the swelling does not press on the flesh;
et met .i. tison ou une tauble desoz l’os por mues coper la char corrumpue;	and place a brand or a knife under the bone to cover the corrupted flesh;
et covient tant soier com on puet veoir et sentir la corruption, et soier ancor autre fois.	and one must see and feel the corruption as much as possible, and do this again and again.
Et se li os est corrumpus, et n’apert mie, et li corruptions est en mileu ou en une partie,	And if the bone is broken, and does not open, and the fracture is in the middle or in one part,
si descuevre la char toute; puis met .i. tison desoz,	exposing all the flesh; then place a burning brand underneath it,
et puis soie des l’une partie a l’autre la corruption, et soit li soieure dou lonc de la corruption .i. poc, si com nos avons dit;	and then sew up the corruption from one end to the other, and let the stitch be as long as the fracture, as we have said;
et se li corruptions est en la jointure, si cope la jointure corrumpue, et soie l’os ou elle contient de l’autre part;	and if the corruption is in the joint, cut through the joint, and sew up the bone on the other side of it;
et se li corruptions est en la continuation des .ij. jointes, si n’i a autre angien que dou coper;	and if the dislocation is at the juncture of the two joints, then there is no need to cover it with anything else;
et se li corruptions est ou poignil de la main, ou ou poignil dou piet, si est mout fort celle chose,	if the dislocation is at the knuckle of the hand or the ankle, then that thing is very serious,
